Greetings from MyWays!

Initiated by a team of IIT Delhi Alumni & incubated by IIM Ahmedabad, MyWays is  an AI based Career Growth Platform that aims at easing the life of students at every step of their career.

Our portal uses a set of AI tools through EPS (Employability Positioning System)  which considers the holistic parameters of a student and helps them find the best suited opportunities customized according to their expertise.

Why is EPS unique ?
 A personalized skill assessment program that identifies the specific skills gap in each student.
 Provides solutions in the form of Curated Learning Pathways on how they can bridge these gaps.
Helps students boost career path journey by recommending best fit milestones.

To get free access to both Assessment & Structured Content Learning, 
Log on to -
https://bit.ly/3qwnqQX


We would be happy to help the students upskill themselves & enroll in & start learning and assessing themselves at NO COST.
